u32* key ^THIo0MnM

for (size_t i = 0; i < 3; i++) {
        // XOR with IV or previous ciphertext block
        for (size_t j = 0; j < 4; j++) {
            buffer[j] = pt[i * 4 + j] ^ currentIV[j];
        }

        // Encrypt the Block
        leaEncrypt(&ct[i * 4], buffer, key, LEA_VERSION);

        // Update IV (current ciphertext block becomes next IV)
        memcpy(currentIV, &ct[i * 4], 4 * sizeof(u32));
    } ^KG67tC28

void leaDecrypt(u32* dst, const u32* src,
                const u32* key, const int LEA_VERSION); ^1FN1yBra


for (size_t i = 0; i < numBlocks; i++) {
    // Decrypt the Block
    leaDecrypt(buffer, &ct[i * blockSize], key, LEA_VERSION);

    // XOR with IV or previous ciphertext block
    for (size_t j = 0; j < blockSize; j++) {
        pt[i * blockSize + j] = buffer[j] ^ currentIV[j];
    }

    // Update IV (current ciphertext block becomes next IV)
    memcpy(currentIV, &ct[i * blockSize], blockSize * sizeof(u32));
} ^t9WJuayg

memcpy ^jtxzTCOn
